000110:     function isAllianceBuildingsMapTarget(target) {
000111:         const container = resolveAllianceMapContainer(target);
000112:         if (isAllianceBuildingsPath()) return true;
000113:         if (!container) return false;
000114:         if (['verband-gebauede-map', 'verband-gebaeude-map'].includes(container.id)) return true;
000115:         if (/(?:gebauede|gebaeude)/i.test(container.id || '') && /map/i.test(container.id || '')) return true;
000116:         const row = container.closest?.('.row') || container.parentElement?.parentElement;
000117:         const table = row?.querySelector?.('table') || null;
000118:         if (!table || !isActiveAllianceContextElement(table)) return false;
000119:         const buildingLinks = table.querySelectorAll?.('a[href*="/buildings/"]')?.length || 0;
000120:         const trainingActions = table.querySelectorAll?.('a.btn-success[href*="/buildings/"], button.btn-success, input.btn-success')?.length || 0;
000121:         return buildingLinks >= 3 && trainingActions >= 1;
000122:     }

022135:     function missionRequirementsNumber(value) {
022136:         const digits = String(value ?? '').replace(/[^0-9-]/g, '');
022137:         const number = Number.parseInt(digits, 10);
022138:         return Number.isFinite(number) ? Math.max(0, number) : 0;
022139:     }

022141:     function missionRequirementsOptionalNumber(value) {
022142:         const text = String(value ?? '').trim();
022143:         if (!/\d/u.test(text)) return null;
022144:         return missionRequirementsNumber(text);
022145:     }

022147:     function missionRequirementsCapacity(min = 0, max = min, known = null) {
022148:         const safeMin = Math.max(0, Number(min) || 0);
022149:         let safeMax = max === null || max === undefined ? null : Math.max(safeMin, Number(max) || 0);
022150:         if (safeMax !== null && !Number.isFinite(safeMax)) safeMax = null;
022151:         const exact = known === true ? true : known === false ? false : safeMax !== null && safeMin === safeMax;
022152:         return { min: safeMin, max: safeMax, known: exact, value: safeMin };
022153:     }

022131:     function missionRequirementsEscapeRegex(value) {
022132:         return String(value || '').replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&');
022133:     }
022134: 
022135:     function missionRequirementsNumber(value) {
022136:         const digits = String(value ?? '').replace(/[^0-9-]/g, '');
022137:         const number = Number.parseInt(digits, 10);
022138:         return Number.isFinite(number) ? Math.max(0, number) : 0;
022139:     }
022140: 
022141:     function missionRequirementsOptionalNumber(value) {
022142:         const text = String(value ?? '').trim();
022143:         if (!/\d/u.test(text)) return null;
022144:         return missionRequirementsNumber(text);
022145:     }
022146: 
022147:     function missionRequirementsCapacity(min = 0, max = min, known = null) {
022148:         const safeMin = Math.max(0, Number(min) || 0);
022149:         let safeMax = max === null || max === undefined ? null : Math.max(safeMin, Number(max) || 0);
022150:         if (safeMax !== null && !Number.isFinite(safeMax)) safeMax = null;
022151:         const exact = known === true ? true : known === false ? false : safeMax !== null && safeMin === safeMax;
022152:         return { min: safeMin, max: safeMax, known: exact, value: safeMin };
022153:     }
022154: 
022155:     function missionRequirementsCapacityText(capacity) {
022156:         const value = missionRequirementsCapacity(capacity?.min ?? capacity?.value ?? 0, capacity?.max, capacity?.known);
022157:         if (value.known || value.max === value.min) return value.min.toLocaleString('en-GB');
022158:         if (value.max === null) return value.min > 0 ? `${value.min.toLocaleString('en-GB')}+` : '?';
022159:         return `${value.min.toLocaleString('en-GB')}–${value.max.toLocaleString('en-GB')}`;

027188:         if (!normalised) {
027189:             gmDeleteValueSafe(SCRIPT.discordWebhookState);
027190:             return '';
027191:         }
027192:         if (!gmSetValueSafe(SCRIPT.discordWebhookState, normalised)) {
027193:             throw new Error('Tampermonkey storage is unavailable.');
027194:         }
027195:         return normalised;
027196:     }
027197: 
027198:     function readDiscordWebhookInput({ save = true } = {}) {
027199:         const input = document.querySelector(`#${SCRIPT.panelId} [data-setting="discord-webhook"]`);
027200:         const raw = String(input?.value || getDiscordWebhookUrl()).trim();
027201:         return save ? saveDiscordWebhookUrl(raw) : normaliseDiscordWebhookUrl(raw);
027202:     }

027208:         if (status) {

028877:     function clearDiscordWebhook() {
028878:         if (!getDiscordWebhookUrl()) {
028879:             setDiscordStatus('No Discord webhook is currently saved.', 'neutral');
028880:             return;
028881:         }
028882:         if (!pageWindow.confirm('Remove the saved Discord webhook from Tampermonkey storage?')) return;

028884:         const input = document.querySelector(`#${SCRIPT.panelId} [data-setting="discord-webhook"]`);
028885:         if (input) input.value = '';
028886:         setDiscordStatus('Saved Discord webhook removed.', 'good');
028887:         showToast('Discord webhook cleared');
028888:     }

029182:     function isNightNow(start, end) {
029183:         const now = new Date();
029184:         const current = now.getHours() * 60 + now.getMinutes();
029185:         const startMin = parseTime(start, 19 * 60);
029186:         const endMin = parseTime(end, 7 * 60);
029187:         if (startMin === endMin) return false;
029188:         if (startMin < endMin) return current >= startMin && current < endMin;
029189:         return current >= startMin || current < endMin;
029190:     }
